   <script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    function image_gallery__swiper() {

        const scrollButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.scrollButton');

        scrollButtons.forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener('click', function() {
                const currentSection = button.closest('section');
                const sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');

                let nextSection = null;


                sections.forEach((section, index) => {
                    if (section === currentSection) {
                        nextSection = sections[index + 1];
                    }
                });

                if (nextSection) {
                    nextSection.scrollIntoView({
                        behavior: 'smooth',
                        block: 'start'
                    });
                }
            });
        });

        const isMobile = window.innerWidth < 768;
        const existingSwiper = document.querySelector(".my-image_gallery__swiper-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU")?.swiper;
        if (existingSwiper) {
            existingSwiper.destroy(true, true);
        }

        var swiper = new Swiper(".my-image_gallery__swiper-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU", {
            loop: true,
            effect: "creative",
            spaceBetween: 0,
            centeredSlides: true,
            initialSlide: 2,
            navigation: {
                nextEl: ".home_slider_next-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU",
                prevEl: ".home_slider_prev-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU",
            },
            keyboard: {
                enabled: true
            },
            creativeEffect: {
                perspective: true,
                prev: {
                    translate: ["-80%", "14vw", -100],
                    rotate: [0, 0, -25],
                    scale: 0.7,
                    origin: "center",
                },
                next: {
                    translate: ["80%", "14vw", -100],
                    rotate: [0, 0, 25],
                    scale: 0.7,
                    origin: "center",
                }
            },
            breakpoints: {
                767.98: {
                    slidesPerView: 1,
                    effect: "slide"
                },
                768: {
                    slidesPerView: 3,
                    effect: "creative"
                }
            },
            on: {
                slideChangeTransitionEnd: function() {
                    if (swiper && swiper.slides) {
                        swiper.update();
                    }
                    removeTabindexFromActiveSlide(this);
                },
                slideChange: function() {
                    removeTabindexFromActiveSlide(this);
                    if (swiper && swiper.slides && swiper.slides.length > 0) {
                        var activeSlide = swiper.slides[swiper.activeIndex];
                        var activeSlideId = activeSlide.getAttribute('data-id');
                        if (activeSlideId) {
                            var matchingElement = document.querySelector(`.thumb-slider-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU .swiper-slide[data-id="${activeSlideId}"]`);
                            if (matchingElement) {
                                document.querySelectorAll('.thumb-slider-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU .swiper-slide.wdt-active').forEach(function(elem) {
                                    elem.classList.remove('wdt-active');
                                });
                                matchingElement.classList.add('wdt-active');
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function removeTabindexFromActiveSlide(swiperInstance) {

        const allSlides = document.querySelectorAll('.my-image_gallery__swiper-template--19562841243830__image_gallery_xpa9cU .swiper-slide');

        allSlides.forEach(slide => {
            if (slide.classList.contains('swiper-slide-active')) {
                slide.removeAttribute('tabindex');
                slide.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(anchor => {
                    anchor.removeAttribute('tabindex');
                });
            } else {
                slide.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
                slide.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(anchor => {
                    anchor.setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
                });
            }
        });
    }
    setTimeout(function(){ image_gallery__swiper(); } , 50);
    document.addEventListener('shopify:block:select', function(event) {
        var blockId = event.detail.blockId;
        image_gallery__swiper();
    });
    document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', function(event) {
        image_gallery__swiper();
    });
});

</script>

<script>
 
 
function updateTextPath(textPathElement) {
  if (!textPathElement || typeof textPathElement.appendChild !== 'function') {
    
    return;
  }

  // Clear existing tspans
  textPathElement.innerHTML = '';

  const iterations = window.innerWidth < 575 ? 9 : 10;

  for (let i = 0; i < iterations; i++) {
    const tspanStar = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "tspan");
    tspanStar.textContent = "*";
    tspanStar.setAttribute("dx", "8");
    tspanStar.setAttribute("style", "font-size: 15px; font-family: Newsreader, serif;");

    const tspanView = document.createElementNS("http://www.w3.org/2000/svg", "tspan");
    tspanView.textContent = "View"; // Replace this with translated string if server-rendered
    tspanView.setAttribute("dx", "5");
    tspanView.setAttribute("style", "font-size: 15px; font-family: Newsreader, serif;");

    textPathElement.appendChild(tspanStar);
    textPathElement.appendChild(tspanView);
  }
}

function observeForTextPaths() {
  const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations, obs) => {
    const textPaths = document.querySelectorAll('textPath, textpath');
    if (textPaths.length > 0) {
      textPaths.forEach((tp) => {
        if (tp instanceof SVGTextPathElement || tp.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'textpath') {
          updateTextPath(tp);
        }
      });
      obs.disconnect(); // Done observing once we found them
    }
  });

  observer.observe(document.body, {
    childList: true,
    subtree: true
  });
}

// Run on DOM ready
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  observeForTextPaths();
});
document.addEventListener('shopify:section:reload', observeForTextPaths());
document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', observeForTextPaths()); 
  document.addEventListener('shopify:section:change', observeForTextPaths()); 
  document.addEventListener('shopify:block:change', observeForTextPaths()); 





  

// Initial call to set up the elements
updateTextPath();

// Update on window resize
window.addEventListener('resize', updateTextPath);

</script>

      
    
  </div>
</div>


</section>
```

<script>
  function initializeRotateScroll() {
    var revealingTextImg = document.querySelector('.revealing-text-img-template--19562841243830__revealing_text_img_7NaybG');
    var stickyImgs = revealingTextImg.querySelectorAll('.sticky-img.rotate-scroll-template--19562841243830__revealing_text_img_7NaybG');
    stickyImgs.forEach((img) => {
      img.style.transform = 'rotate(10deg)';
    });

    var targetClass = 'reveal-text';
    var additionalClass = 'revealed';

    var targetClass1 = 'revealing-text-img-template--19562841243830__revealing_text_img_7NaybG';
    var upClass = 'revealed';
    let lastScrollTop = 0;

    function isElementInView(element) {
      var windowTop = $(window).scrollTop();
      var windowBottom = windowTop + $(window).height();
      var elementTop = element.offset().top;
      var elementBottom = elementTop + element.outerHeight();

      return elementBottom > windowTop && elementTop < windowBottom;
    }
    function isElementInView1(element) {
      var windowTop = $(window).scrollTop();
      var windowBottom = windowTop + $(window).height();
      var elementTop = element.offset().top;
      var elementBottom = elementTop + element.outerHeight();

      return elementBottom > windowTop && elementTop < windowBottom;
    }

    window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
      $('.' + targetClass).each(function () {
        if (isElementInView($(this))) {
          $(this).addClass(additionalClass);
        }
      });

      var currentScroll = $(this).scrollTop();
      var isScrollingUp = currentScroll < lastScrollTop;

      $('.' + targetClass).each(function () {
        if (isElementInView1($(this))) {
          if (isScrollingUp) {
            $(this).addClass(upClass);
            
          } else {
            
          }
        }
      });

      lastScrollTop = currentScroll;

      var rect = revealingTextImg.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (rect.top < window.innerHeight && rect.bottom >= 0) {
        var scrollPosition = window.scrollY - rect.top;
        var maxScroll = revealingTextImg.scrollHeight - window.innerHeight;
        var scrollFraction = scrollPosition / maxScroll;

        stickyImgs.forEach((img) => {
          var rotationDegree = 10 + scrollFraction * 360;
          img.style.transform = `rotate(${rotationDegree}deg)`;
        });
      }
    });
  }
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    function initializeRotateScroll() {
      var revealingTextImg = document.querySelector('.revealing-text-img-template--19562841243830__revealing_text_img_7NaybG');
      var stickyImgs = revealingTextImg.querySelectorAll('.sticky-img.rotate-scroll-template--19562841243830__revealing_text_img_7NaybG');
      stickyImgs.forEach((img) => {
        img.style.transform = 'rotate(10deg)';
      });

      var targetClass = 'reveal-text';
      var additionalClass = 'revealed';

      var targetClass1 = 'revealing-text-img-template--19562841243830__revealing_text_img_7NaybG';
      var upClass = 'revealed';
      let lastScrollTop = 0;

      function isElementInView(element) {
        var windowTop = $(window).scrollTop();
        var windowBottom = windowTop + $(window).height();
        var elementTop = element.offset().top;
        var elementBottom = elementTop + element.outerHeight();

        return elementBottom > windowTop && elementTop < windowBottom;
      }
      function isElementInView1(element) {
        var windowTop = $(window).scrollTop();
        var windowBottom = windowTop + $(window).height();
        var elementTop = element.offset().top;
        var elementBottom = elementTop + element.outerHeight();

        return elementBottom > windowTop && elementTop < windowBottom;
      }

      window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        $('.' + targetClass).each(function () {
          if (isElementInView($(this))) {
            $(this).addClass(additionalClass);
          }
        });

        var currentScroll = $(this).scrollTop();
        var isScrollingUp = currentScroll < lastScrollTop;

        $('.' + targetClass).each(function () {
          if (isElementInView1($(this))) {
            if (isScrollingUp) {
              $(this).addClass(upClass);
              
            } else {
              
            }
          }
        });

        lastScrollTop = currentScroll;

        var rect = revealingTextImg.getBoundingClientRect();
        if (rect.top < window.innerHeight && rect.bottom >= 0) {
          var scrollPosition = window.scrollY - rect.top;
          var maxScroll = revealingTextImg.scrollHeight - window.innerHeight;
          var scrollFraction = scrollPosition / maxScroll;

          stickyImgs.forEach((img) => {
            var rotationDegree = 10 + scrollFraction * 360;
            img.style.transform = `rotate(${rotationDegree}deg)`;
          });
        }
      });
    }
    initializeRotateScroll();
  });
  if (Shopify.designMode) {
    document.addEventListener('shopify:section:load', initializeRotateScroll);
    document.addEventListener('shopify:section:reorder', initializeRotateScroll);
    document.addEventListener('shopify:section:select', initializeRotateScroll);
  }
</script> 


</section>
```
